  PRIMARY KEY  (`cartItemsID`)
) TYPE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=4709 ;

-- Table structure for table `nameDef`

  `description` mediumtext NOT NULL,
  `display_color` varchar(6) NOT NULL default '',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`nameID`)
) TYPE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=41 ;

  `name` varchar(20) NOT NULL default '',
  `value` varchar(20) NOT NULL default '',

) TYPE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=3 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- 
-- Table structure for table `receipts`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `receipts` (
  `BuyerID` bigint(20) NOT NULL default '0',
  `UserID` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `OrderNumber` bigint(20) NOT NULL default '0',
  `Date` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
